They accept Care Credit which is a plus, and they have Saturday appointments which make my life much easier. Scheduling and rescheduling are fairly convenient and I know that my cats are in excellent hands. At times, the wait time once you get into the exam room can be a little lengthy, but I feel that‚Äôs how any doctors office is. They always seem to have parking for their customers/clients even on the busy Mission Blvd and though their building is pretty old and could use an upgrade, their veterinarian knows his stuff. The receptionists are adequate, but could be more professional. Overall the convenience outweighs everything else.<//review>

They have the best carnitas in the Bay Area that I've found, juicy, flavorful with a delicious piquancy.  With a change in ownership in 2017 I was scared, but the new owners have done the original founders proud.  The food is still magnificent, and several modernizations have spruced up the place. < text>
To Start: Just Exceptional!

My wife and I travel full time. When we are on the road, lots of things go wrong. Tires are the one thing that make me cringe because automatically, I know it's going to be expensive. Living on the road full-time, also opens the door for businesses to take advantage of that situation. They know you are in a hurry to get back on the road, or that services aren't always plentiful, or that time is of the essence and money speeds things up.

Lance: The Rockstar!

We were mid road trip, and noticed a bulge on a sidewall of our SUV. The tires were about due anyways, but trying to hold onto every last mile, put us in a world of panic. Not knowing if the tire would even make it another mile, and dead in our tracks, we called here as the closest trustworthy tire shop to our location. Lance went above and beyond what my wildest expectations were. He got a set of 4 special order tires in - THE SAME DAY - which saved us a ton of time waiting and not traveling.

When we got there, everything was ready and waiting including telling me about some more discounts that were available to me rather than jacking up the prices and making me pay more. He even beat the the lowest price listed online, for the tires alone, by a few bucks which really made us happy.

This is why I have been an America's/Discount Tire Co customer for over 20 years exclusively. This, right here. My wife and I were so blown away at the level of service and care, we bought the entire store lunch to show our true appreciation for what they were able to do for us. The time and money they saved us, was worth well over the monetary cost of lunch.

Thank you! For everything!</text>

< Review>
You really have to try a little bit of everything here to truly appreciate the quality of the food. Perhaps trying the "fruits of the sea platter" would be a good way to start. The tuna also excellent but my favorite would probably have to be the Alaskan Halibut.  This place is a fish lovers paradise. Like most fine restaurants the portions at Water Grill are extremely small. You have to have a five course meal to fill your stomach and enjoy your dining experience. The five course meals can get extremely pricey, but you do get what you pay for. The arraignment of the food on the plate seems carefully crafted. I was tempted to lick my plate clean, but it probably would not have been appropriate at a fancy place like this. The desert was excellent and carefully crafted as well.

If money is no concern, you should not be disappointed here.<//Review>

In the heart of the city off Grand Ave. You will find this upscale working-class hero. <user_name>David Campbell</user_name><time>1600076470460</time>< rating>

< text>
This little nugget was very hard to find as it is located in what seems to be an office building with a few restaurants like Olive Garden and California Pizza Kitchen. We almost turned around due to the fact that not only did it take us about 10 minutes to find the place, but the above mentioned restaurants are such a turnoff, that we thought SS could not be all that great despite the amazing reviews. Boy, were we WRONG!
I have to point out that when you enter the door, there is a sign prominently displayed by the cash register that makes it clear california rolls, spicy tuna rolls, and etc are NOT an option! Upon reading that, I knew that we were in for a treat as this to me meant that this was a serious and authentic sushi restaurant.
Wanting to be adventuresome, we sat at the sushi bar where you are not provided with a menu, as the options are the chefs choice. We had some amazing creations and I have to say that this was the best experience and the best sushi that I have ever had. So worth every penny!< /text>

<Name>Kera Periwinkle<//Name>< Time>
1545041624243<//Time>
< Rating>
3<//Rating>
<Text>I made a reservation here for my ninth anniversary with my husband and he loved it but he's not the one writing this review, now is he?  First, we both love seafood- he more than I, which is why I chose this place versus my first choice, French food.

I wasn't a fan of the decor.  It felt like it was dusty and hadn't been fully cleaned in a while, like the smudgy glass and all.  It felt like I was stuck in some outdated restaurant from the 80s, which I think is when they first opened, so that description is actually appropriate.

Ambience was okay.  It was a pricier, more upscale place but it didn't feel snooty or unwelcoming.  Our server was on top of it; he was quick, knowledgable and friendly.  Everyone was really nice, so I feel bad about just leaving a three-star "A-OK" rating but I just was not about the food at all.

Our dinner:
-Wild Alaskan Black Cod Kabayaki (Sablefish) with soba noodles, green onions, spiced fish broth
-Wild Ross Sea Chilean Sea Bass with butternut squash pur√©e, gnocchi, sage brown butter
-Jumbo Lump Blue Crab Cake with celery root remoulade
-Bread Pudding a la mode with sea salt caramel ice cream

Both fish dishes were cooked to perfection- the right amount of crisp and flakiness with such a fresh taste.  However, the Wild Alaskan Black Cod Kabayaki was too salty for me and I hated the butternut squash pur√©e on my Wild Ross Sea Chilean Sea Bass.  I don't like butternut squash much in general but when it's paired right, it can be very delicious.  I thought that the sea bass was just soaking in way too much of the pur√©e and it just overwhelmed the dish.  My husband loves butternut squash and even he thought it was heavy-handed on that sauce.

I don't know why I bothered with the Jumbo Lump Blue Crab Cake.  I've never in my life had a decent crab cake yet I feel the need to order it every time I see it on a menu, with this ridiculous hope that someone will actually get it right and that it will be outstanding.  This was not that time.

The Bread Pudding was complimentary for our anniversary, which was a sweet touch (no pun intended).  It was the BEST bread pudding I've ever had but... I don't like bread pudding.  It's very reminiscent of a White convalescent home, much like carrot cake and split pea soup.  No, thank you.

Honestly, the best part of the dinner for me was the warm, chewy sour dough bread.  It was absolutely delicious and I could just eat that all night.

If my husband were to write this review, he would undoubtedly give this place a solid four, if not five, stars.  I wish I could do the same.<//Text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPX7-DP07mvQQSxDjDjuOVYj9HlQ2bvNJ_EEZYW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPyX-4R4XONYdCZv46V-U72nQVEy1e-T9g5mvvF=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM1I64uVCBLMQq6TDqJsAOXJPlvZXQnjdbehtup=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNOhse673mikUJB0qAujfEQNw0Zqg4nYQjMZ-f_=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOkKLEyRIdC3BZeIkoNATOKEuZxrM4Aul4Etl5h=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures>< resp>

<rating>4< /rating>< text>
Initially I was skeptical because from the outside, it looked pretty basic like a sandwich shop. Once we got inside and were seated, I was pleasantly surprised by the lit candle, smooth mood with dimmed lights, and prompt service. We had a couple of pasta dishes with seafood in it. We were really lucky to stop in at the right time. We will definitely go back.< /text>

In the mood for a mouth-watering meal? You've come to the right place with Versailles!

AMBIANCE (4/5)
Homey, large with lots of tables, no-frills, casual. Good for groups.

<rate>5<//rate>< text>
To begin, the atmosphere is elegant and beautiful. It is definitely more of a place for adults than families with young kids, but they do have something for everyone. All of the food we had was of very high quality, and it all tasted delicious. However, service was a bit slow and nothing was mind-blowing. In a city of such diverse food and dining opportunities, this restaurant would not be the first to mind when recommending incredible seafood. (hint: try Son of a Gun on W 3rd Street). Watergrill can be found and enjoyed in a lot of places; it is not a unique hidden gem. If you are looking for a beautiful meal in downtown LA, this is a good choice. If you are looking for a revolutionary meal in Los Angeles, I would maybe try elsewhere. Watergrill is always solid and delivers consistently good meals.<//text>

< Text>
Water Grill is a legacy DTLA restaurant for seafood. I visited during Dine LA week and ordered off that menu. I enjoyed a delicious beet salad and a fish main dish. The service is superb here -- actually, I like the service more than the food. It's also a good place for a business lunch or a special lunch with a friend because unlike a lot of other restaurants, the noise level is low. It's a bit pricey, but worth it for a business lunch or special meal.</Text>

<review>We went to Water Grill after attending the opera at the Dorothy Chandler Pavilion  last Sunday.  Water Grill is located just a couple blocks south of the Dorothy Chandler Pavilion so getting there was a breeze.  Parking was very easy in the valet parking garage located next to and just north of the restaurant.  We were seated at a table but asked to move to a booth which they accommodated kindly.  Service and food was excellent.  The prices are a bit steep but, hey it's downtown LA and the selection of food makes up for it in comparison to some of the other local fancy restaurants.  We were celebrating a birthday and it was quite a treat to get a complimentary bread pudding we had read so much about.  The food was good but the bread pudding was truly amazing and the highlight of the meal.  I would definitely recommend it!</review><rating>4</rating></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
The atmosphere made me feel like we'd stepped off the busy streets of a modern Los Angeles into a different time. The place is welcoming and comfortable.  The homedmade fresh breads are both delicious and served while you wait for your food.  We shared a sampler platter of oysters and each one was unique and fresh.  The prices are comparitive to other fresh seafood restaurants across the country, but the food quality and service are superior.  The Water Grill is a must go place in the sea of cuisine in the downtown area.  I will definitely go here again when I return and I'll share the bowl of clam chowder.<//Review>

I love seafood and decided to try this restaurant with three friends during DineLA week.  We had a reservation for lunch on a Sunday.  I tried the clam chowder which was very bland. I'm not one to have to add salt to my food, however, I felt like couldn't add enough!  We each ordered the salmon; when it came out it looked dry.  It tasted like rubber.  It wasn't just my dish, but all four of us! It was small lunch portions and no one could not finish it.  The waitress asked us about our food and we told her it tasted was overcooked, reheated, or something.  She offered to replace our portions however we declined.  Since it was a dineLA promotion (to attract new patrons), we were not going to make a huge deal.  We just paid our bill and decided we would not eat there again or recommend it.  The waitress was nice enough to bring us bread pudding dessert on the house.  It was only okay.  I was very disappointed since there were rave reviews about this restaurant.<//text>

<pictures>None< /pictures><resp>None<//resp><Rate>4</Rate>< Text>
Water Grill has a cool, moody atmosphere that probably makes it equally good for business and romance. I've been a few times for Restaurant Week and have come to realize that I vastly prefer ordering their cold seafood platters over the cooked fish filet dishes. Somehow I think the straightforward presentations of quality oysters, mussels, shrimp, etc on the cold platters are more satisfying than a more staid filet.

Unexpected bonus: the table bread is freshly baked and shockingly good. (Hint: ask your server nicely for extra bread!)</Text>

Was ok. Expensive being fine dining. But food didn't surprise me.</Text>
<pictures>None<//pictures><response>{'time': 1561575879803, 'text': "We're so sorry to have missed the mark.  We hope to wow you next time!"}< /response><gmapID>0x80c2c7b4901ce7c7:0x2ad996c9a82b097c< /gmapID></record>

<gmap_id>0x80c2c7b4901ce7c7:0x2ad996c9a82b097c< /gmap_id><Rate>4< /Rate><pics>None< /pics>< text>
Delicious, tingly sparking water. That's how I would describe the Water Grill revamp. This DTLA classic recently remodeled, and a little nip-tuck sure does a classic place some good! Just like water, a classic, the water grill sometimes gets overlooked for some new hipster joints in the historic core of DTLA, or the latest and greatest modern-ish spots, but with the new facelift and revamed menu, it is like classics-revamped.... like sparkling water.

The interior is now open, almost like an East Coast seafood bar, with the day's catch displayed for your oogling and picking pleasure. They have oysters, clams, scallops on the half shell, all uniquely prepared, and ready for you at lunch. It's much more open, and feels less now like an old school steakhouse, which, to me, is great if you are eating steak at night, with the mafia bosses next to you. Not as great for an upscale, but still casual, business lunch. I think the decor and everything now is perfect.

The service, as always, remains impeccable.

What really surpised me the last few visits, though, was how great the food has become. I remember being very let down the first time I came, and vowing never to pay that much for eh-eh seafood again. Luckily, work brought me here and I've come around and changed my mind about this place.

My favorites:
-WHOLE STEAMED LOBSTER, served with drawn butter. These are Maine Lobsters (giant, succulent claws) and so delicious. They come pre-cracked, so it isn't SO messy for a business lunch. They also offer you bibs, and to "bib you" and "de-bib you". Cute sidenote: the bibs have fishing buoys for all the fisherman the restaurant has ever worked with, even those who have passed on (including the grandfathers of the founders!).
-WILD MORRO BAY BLACK COD pan saut√©ed with tomato jam and seasonal succotash. When i had this AMAZING dish, it was served with sea bass instead as a daily special. if this is available, GET IT. the tomato jam is perfect compliment, to a seared fish, and the -succotash is just enough to give some character to the dish. it was delightful.
-CLAM CHOWDER: took an East Coast client here, and they said the clam chowder was some of the best they'd ever had! Includes whole clams, 4 on the shell, looks great, and tastes wonderful. Not so thick-chowdery, but still creamy and delicious.

Wonderful dtla business lunch addition. Will be back, often, especially if it is on the company dime!<//text>

I think I missed my calling of being an executive working in DTLA because as such, I would lunch everyday at the WG.

Once again, DineLA brought me to this establishment, that had been high on my to dine list, which I never seemed to get around to, but finally did.  And, so glad I did.

<review>I was impressed with the Water Grill! It is now my favorite seafood restaurant aside from The Lobster.

To start we shared an iced platter of 6 oysters (kumamoto, wianno, chef's creek),  sea urchin, peruvian bay scallops, and jumbo white shrimp. It was delicious! A second round was ordered. WG definitely knows how to bring their A-game serving up the freshest from of the sea.

For our main course we had the chilean seabass served with butternut squash gnocchi. The fish was so moist and buttery, definitely one of the best I've had. The gnocchi had great texture and excellent flavors as well.
The filet mignon was tender and cooked perfectly as requested but could use a bit more salt.

There were no room left for dessert as we were stuffed.

Overall, a terrific time and amazing food. Can't wait to be back!< /review><Pictures>None<//Pictures><Response>None</Response>< gmap_id>
